mame2010 per-game audio class list
======================================================================

WHAT THE CLASSES MEAN
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Unlike mame2003, every emulated sound chip in mame2010 runs its stream at
its own native rate and the stream mixer resamples each to the core output
rate. So the useful question is how many DISTINCT native rates a game has:
if there is only one, the core can set its output rate to that rate and the
mixer becomes a 1:1 copy (resample-free); the frontend then performs the
single conversion to the host rate.

Sound sources are bucketed as:
  class 1 (output rate): synthesizes directly at the core output rate, so it
    never forces a resample. (SAMPLES, SN76477, SPEAKER, and the FILTER_*
    pass-throughs.)
  class 2 (native rate) : runs at a fixed clock-derived rate. (Almost every
    chip: AY8910 clk/8, YM2151 clk/64, OPL/YM3812/YM3526/Y8950 clk/72,
    YM2413 clk/72, OKIM6295 clk/divisor, SEGAPCM clk/128, K007232 clk/128,
    RF5C68/RF5C400 clk/384, YMF271 clk/384, YMF278B clk/768, UPD7759 clk/4,
    IREMGA20 clk/4, TMS5220/5100 clk/80, the FM cores at their FM rate,
    fixed-rate cores SCSP/AICA/CDDA 44100, PSXSPU 44100, YMZ280B internal,
    GAELCO 8000, etc.)
  special               : DISCRETE netlists and the custom/CPU sound cores
    (LASERDISC, AMIGA, LELAND/REDLINE_80186, CPS3, SNES, PHOENIX, SNK6502,
    SEIBU_ADPCM ...) whose effective rate is driver/runtime dependent.

Per game we bucket on the count of DISTINCT class-2 (type,clock) sources:
  NONE    - 0 class-2 sources             -> already resample-free
  SINGLE  - exactly 1 class-2 native rate -> output AT that rate, resample-free
  MULTI   - >=2 distinct class-2 sources  -> some resampling unavoidable
  SPECIAL - only special/custom sources   -> rate is driver dependent
A '+SPECIAL' tag marks SINGLE/MULTI games that also carry a special source.

RATE POLICY
----------------------------------------------------------------------
SINGLE games should set the core output rate to the chip's native rate so the
mixer never resamples; the frontend performs the one conversion to the host
rate. NONE games are resample-free at any output rate. MULTI and SPECIAL
games follow the 'Sample Rate' core option.

SUMMARY (of 8892 games)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  NONE    (resample-free) .......   390
  SINGLE  (one native rate) .....  4758
  MULTI   (resampling) ..........  3235
  SPECIAL (driver dependent) ....   509
